5 import play.api._

24 /**
25  * This Controller handles API Requests concerning events
26  */
27 class EventController @Inject()(cc: ControllerComponents,
28                                 protected val dbConfigProvider: DatabaseConfigProvider,
29                                 val silhouette: Silhouette[AuthEnv],
30                                 val organizerService: OrganizerService,
31                                 val userService: UserService,
32                                 eventService: EventService,
33                                 locationService: LocationService)
34     (implicit context: ExecutionContext)
35     extends AbstractController(cc)
36     with HasDatabaseConfigProvider[JdbcProfile]
37     with Util {
38 
39   val log = Logger("api.event")
40 
41   def getEvent(id: Int) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
42     log.debug("Rest request to get event")
43 
44     val q = for(e <- EventTable.event if e.id === id.bind) yield e;
45 
46     db.run(q.detailed).map(x => x.headOption match {
47       case Some(r) => Ok(Json.toJson(r))
48       case _ => NotFound
49     })
50   }
51 
52   def searchEvents(search: Option[String], location: Option[Int], category: Option[Int],
53                    sort: Option[String], sortDir: Boolean, from: Option[Timestamp], to: Option[Timestamp]) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
54     log.debug("Rest request to search events")
55     
56     val q = for {
57       e <- event if similar(e.name,search.getOrElse("").bind) || search.getOrElse("").bind === ""
58                  if e.categories.filter(_.id === category.getOrElse(-1)).exists || category.getOrElse(-1).bind === -1
59                  if e.locationId - location.getOrElse(-1).bind === 0 || location.getOrElse(-1).bind === -1
60                  if e.from >= from.getOrElse(new Timestamp(0,0,0,0,0,0,0)) && e.from <= to.getOrElse(new Timestamp(4000,0,0,0,0,0,0))
61                  if e.to.getOrElse(plus(e.from,oneDay)) >= currentTimestamp
62     } yield e
63 
64     val s = q.sortColumn(sort,sortDir).queryPaged.detailed
65     returnPaged(s,q,db)
66   }
67 
68   def getNearby(id: Int) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
69     log.debug("Rest request to get events nearby another event")
70 
71     val q = for(e <- EventTable.event if e.id === id.bind) yield e;
72 
73     db.run(q.detailed).map(_.headOption).flatMap {
74       case Some(e) => {
75         val q = EventTable.event.join(LocationTable.location).on(_.locationId === _.id)
76           .sortBy(y => geoDistance(e.location.latitude.getOrElse(0.0f).bind, e.location.longitude.getOrElse(0.0f).bind, 
77               y._2.latitude.getOrElse(0.0f), y._2.longitude.getOrElse(0.0f)))
78           .map(_._1).filter(y => y.id =!= e.id && y.from >= currentTimestamp)
79         val s = q.queryPaged.detailed
80         returnPaged(s,q,db)
81       }
82       case None => Future(NotFound)
83     }
84   }
85 
86   def getSameViewed(id: Int) = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
87     log.debug("Rest request to get events other participants also visit")
88 
89     val q = ParticipantCountView.participantCount.filter(_.id === id.bind)
90       .join(EventTable.event).on(_.event_fk === _.id)
91       .sortBy(y => y._1.count.desc).map(_._2)
92       .filter(y => y.id =!= id.bind && y.from >= currentTimestamp)
93 
94     val s = q.queryPaged.detailed
95 
96     returnPaged(s,q,db)
97   }
98 
99   def deleteEvent(id: Int) = organizerRequest(parse.default) { (request,organizer) =>
100     log.debug("Rest request to get event")
101 
102     val q = event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind && x.creatorId === organizer.id).delete
103 
104     db.run(q).map {
105       case 0 => NotFound
106       case x => Ok(Json.toJson(x))
107     }
108   }
109 
110   def createEvent() = organizerRequest(parse.json) { case (request,organizer) =>
111     EventForm.form.bindFromRequest()(request).fold(
112       form => {
113         Future.successful(BadRequest(Json.toJson(form.errors)))
114       },
115       data => {
116         log.debug("Rest request to create event")
117 
118         val location = locationService.insertOrGet(data.location)
119 
120         val imagesQuery = DBIO.sequence(data.images.map(x => ImageTable.image.filter(_.id === x.id.bind).result.map(l => l.map(r => (r,x.tag))))).map(_.flatten)
121 
122         val categoriesQuery = DBIO.sequence(
123           data.categories.map {
124             case cat =>
125               cat.id match {
126                 case None => insertAndReturn[Category,CategoryTable](CategoryTable.category,cat).map(x => List(x).seq)
127                 case Some(id) => CategoryTable.category.filter(_.id === id.bind).result
128               }
129           }).map(_.flatten)
130 
131         db.run(imagesQuery.zip(categoriesQuery)).zip(location).flatMap {
132           case ((images,categories),Some(location)) => {
133             val event = Event(None, data.name, data.from, data.to,
134                               data.description, data.shortDescription,
135                               organizer.id, location.id.getOrElse(-1),
136                               data.priceMin, data.priceMax)
137             db.run(insertAndReturn[Event,EventTable](EventTable.event,event)).map(r => (r,images,categories))
138           }.flatMap { case (event,images,categories) =>
139               val imagesAdd = ImageEntityTable.imageEntity ++= images.map(img => ImageEntity(img._1.id.getOrElse(-1),event.id.getOrElse(-1),EntityType.Event,img._2))
140               val categoriesAdd = EventCategoryTable.eventCategory ++= categories.map(cat => (cat.id.getOrElse(-1),event.id.getOrElse(-1)))
141               val eventDetailed = EventTable.event.filter(_.id === event.id.getOrElse(-1)).detailed
142               db.run(imagesAdd.zip(categoriesAdd) >> eventDetailed)
143           }.map(x => Ok(Json.toJson(x.head)))
144           case _ => Future.successful(BadRequest)
145         }
146       })
147   }
148 
149   def updateEvent(id: Int) = organizerRequest(parse.json) { case (request,organizer) =>
150     EventForm.form.bindFromRequest()(request).fold(
151       form => {
152         Future.successful(BadRequest(Json.toJson(form.errors)))
153       },
154       data => {
155         log.debug("Rest request to update event")
156 
157         val location = locationService.insertOrGet(data.location)
158 
159         val imagesQuery = DBIO.sequence(data.images.map(x => ImageTable.image.filter(_.id === x.id.bind).result.map(l => l.map(r => (r,x.tag))))).map(_.flatten)
160 
161         val categoriesQuery = DBIO.sequence(
162           data.categories.map {
163             case cat =>
164               cat.id match {
165                 case None => insertAndReturn[Category,CategoryTable](CategoryTable.category,cat).map(x => List(x).seq)
166                 case Some(id) => CategoryTable.category.filter(_.id === id.bind).result
167               }
168           }).map(_.flatten)
169 
170         val eventQuery = EventTable.event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind && x.creatorId === organizer.id).result.map(_.headOption)
171 
172         db.run(imagesQuery.zip(categoriesQuery).zip(eventQuery)).zip(location).flatMap {
173           case (((images,categories),Some(event)),Some(location)) => {
174             val event = Event(Some(id), data.name, data.from, data.to,
175                               data.description, data.shortDescription,
176                               organizer.id, location.id.getOrElse(-1),
177                               data.priceMin, data.priceMax)
178 
179             val getQuery = EventTable.event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind && x.creatorId === organizer.id)
180 
181             db.run(getQuery.update(event) >> getQuery.result.map(_.head))
182               .map(r => Some((r,images,categories)))
183           }
184           case _ => Future.successful(None)
185         }.flatMap {
186           case Some((event,images,categories)) => {
187             val dropImages = ImageEntityTable.imageEntity.filter(x => x.entityId === id && x.entityType === EntityType.Event).delete
188             val dropCategories = EventCategoryTable.eventCategory.filter(x => x.eventID === id).delete
189             val dropQuery = dropImages.zip(dropCategories)
190 
191             val imagesAdd = ImageEntityTable.imageEntity ++= images.map(img => ImageEntity(img._1.id.getOrElse(-1),event.id.getOrElse(-1),EntityType.Event, img._2))
192             val categoriesAdd = EventCategoryTable.eventCategory ++= categories.map(cat => (cat.id.getOrElse(-1),event.id.getOrElse(-1)))
193             val eventDetailed = EventTable.event.filter(_.id === event.id.getOrElse(-1)).detailed
194             db.run(dropQuery >> imagesAdd.zip(categoriesAdd) >> eventDetailed).map(x => Some(x))
195           }
196           case None => Future.successful(None)
197         }.map {
198           case Some(e) => Ok(Json.toJson(e))
199           case None => BadRequest
200         }
201       })
202   }
203 
204   def insertCSV = organizerRequest(parse.multipartFormData) { case (request,organizer) =>
205     log.debug("Rest request to insert events by csv")
206 
207     request.body.file("csv").map { case x =>
208       val file = x.ref.path.toFile()
209 
210       eventService.insertCSV(file,organizer)
211      }.map(_.map(x => Ok(Json.toJson(x)))).headOption.getOrElse(Future.successful(BadRequest))
212   }
213 
214   def participate(id: Int) = userRequest(parse.default) { case (request,user) =>
215     log.debug("Rest request to participate in event")
216 
217     val q = (event.filter(x => x.id === id.bind).result)
218       .zip(ParticipantTable.participant.filter(x => x.eventID === id.bind && x.userID === user.id.getOrElse(-1).bind).result)
219 
220     db.run(q).map(x => (x._1.headOption,x._2.headOption)).flatMap {
221       case (Some(e),None) => {
222         db.run(ParticipantTable.participant += ((user.id.getOrElse(-1),id)))
223         Future.successful(Ok)
224       }
225       case (Some(e),Some(p)) => Future.successful(Conflict)
226       case (None,_) => Future.successful(BadRequest)
227     }
228   }
229 
230   def unparticipate(id: Int) = userRequest(parse.default) { case (request,user) =>
231     log.debug("Rest request to unparticipate in event")
232 
233     db.run(ParticipantTable.participant.filter(x => x.eventID === id.bind && x.userID === user.id.getOrElse(-1).bind).delete)
234       .flatMap {
235       case 1 => {
236         Future.successful(Ok)
237       }
238       case _ => Future.successful(BadRequest)
239     }
240   }

243   def getSliderEvents = Action.async { implicit request: Request[AnyContent] =>
244     log.debug("Rest request to get events for slider")
245 
246     db.run(SliderEventTable.sliderEvent.sortBy(_.number).flatMap(_.event).detailed).map(x => Ok(Json.toJson(x)))
247   }
